< text>
I found MySpaCover online looking for the dimensions of my particular hot tub. The website has a handle make and model look up that will pre-populate the dimensions needed for your spa since they are building the covers from scratch. You then are walked though many different customizations like thickness, vapor barriers, tapers and color. I purchased the Premium Energy Saver with Heat Seal and Double Wrapped Core. The ordering experience was great and after placing my order, my wife said we should get a different color. Changing the color was easy with their online chat feature (changed from rust to walnut).

When the cover arrive it fit perfectly on my spa and looks great too! When you lift the cover using the spa handle its kind of hard at first because of the great airtight seal that is formed which is a good thing for energy efficiency. Basically the cover is vacuum sealed on the spa saving energy and allowing me to keep it hot longer.

The only downside was the wait for the cover. That's probably because I am spoiled with amazon prime 2 day delivery. We ordered this cover on April 2 and received on May 10. Because this cover is fabricated from scratch (I believe in Mexico), it takes longer than I am used to waiting for things. Also you are not given a UPS tracking number in your order which makes you worry a little bit. However, each time I emailed the customer service I was given a status update on my order.

I highly recommend ordering your next spa cover from MySpaCover for both quality, the ability to customize the cover their customer service.< /text>

<Time>1542297359268<//Time><Rating>5<//Rating><Text>Well it was October, and I realized that our hot tub cover was simply not up to another Western PA winter. So I went to my local hot tub vendor to order a replacement cover. They said they couldn't deliver for 6 weeks! But they would check on the price and see if a better delivery was available. They came back to me with a proposal of $500 and 8 weeks (losing ground here, fellows).

Luckily, I got a proposal from My Spa Cover while I was waiting for my local vendor. $400 and 3 weeks delivered. Guess which cover I ordered. Even if My Spa Cover was 2 weeks late, I would still be ahead of the game.

So I got the measurements on my old cover (my My Spa Cover rep made sure she had all of the measurements she needed before she would finalize the order) and I placed the order. When I placed the order, she assured me that the product would ship in 2 weeks and it would take a week for ground shipping. Well, OK, we'll see.

The replacement cover was at my door exactly 3 weeks (to the day!) after the order was placed. And it was delivered in perfect condition.

When I opened the shipping box, I checked every measurement - every one was exactly as I had given to My Spa Cover.

We pulled the old cover off the tub and spotted the new one onto it, installation was complete in about 10 minutes. A few notes:
-	The new cover comes in a very large box. Not terribly heavy (about 60 lb.), but very awkward. I found it helpful to have some help to remove the old cover and place the new one in position.
-	The new cover is noticeably thicker than the old one. Since these covers are all typically made of the same materials, I took this to mean that the new cover was going to save me energy on heat.
-	The new cover is quite a bit lighter than the old one. I suspect the old cover was waterlogged. I probably should have replaced it a couple of years ago.
-	Since the old cover was so heavy, I needed to slice through its hinge so I could carry it in two pieces. This also makes friends with the trash man when he takes the old one away.

All in all, I am very pleased with this entire purchase, from the specification before fabrication, through their rapid construction and shipping, and the very good quality of the delivered product. I would definitely purchase from this company again.</Text>< Pictures>

<UserId.>111305349157313600862</UserId.><username>Bryan<//username><Date>1542325198528<//Date><Rating>5</Rating>< text>
First here!

Playpie has been my anticipated go to business for toddlers and kids , because of the convenience of the location and the environment.

This Family friendly/kid friendly indoor playground consists of state of the art brand new playground equipments and books for all.

It is scheduled to open on November 18th, 2018 (Sunday) and I have been eyeing the opening of the business for past several months.

I'm solely submitting this review on the business's LOCATION, CONVENIENCE, PRICE, AND VALUE.

Location is great. Its inside OC source mall (Near Beach Blvd and Orangethorpe) which is predominantly Korean businesses with Korean employees, but nobody judges here other than maybe employees speaking English less fluently?

Parking is FREE....FREE!!!  Cant get better than that. All day, everyday. It gets crowded during weekends, but it has 4 floors plus the roof parking , and elevator located in every floor along with steps, you really can't complain.

Price is what i expected. It runs $16.95 for toddlers over 2, $10.95 for 1-2 year olds, under 1 is free, and every adult pays $4.95.
So parents of a 1 child should cost you the all day pass with re-Entry for around $29-30 including tax.
That's all day entry, so you can let kids play, go out and eat and comeback if you wanted to for that price. That is a bargain and a great business strategy in my mind.
Not sure if they might change that near future, but lets just hope they keep it that way.

They DO NOT have inside kitchen or food court,  but they have catering menu for birthday parties and for kids events.
The staff i spoke with confirmed that they will roll out catering menu and they have certain vendors they work with, so they will bring the food to your reserved room for the day.

The value in overall seems great and better than near by indoor playgrounds, since 90% of them were built long time ago and doesn't have the fancy+newer equipments that Playpie offers.

They also have gender neutral restroom, not sure if they have a diaper changing station, but will post updated review after my initial visit soon.
I usually take my baby girl to Billy Beez, but it gets super crowded during weekends and there are like middle school kids pushing little ones,  so you gotta consider those factors too.

Like I mentioned at the beginning of the review, this business is not opened yet, so the review excludes customer service, staff friendliness,  how staff handles issues, and customer quality. After all, not trying to be rude but you just want safe environment and people around your kid as a parent. Nobody wants bullies, homeless, rude people, cursing, hitting, and etc when youre kid is playing.

I will post updated review after initial visit within 2 weeks. Also more detailed pics inside.
Stay tuned!<//text>

< userid>
102220085079793311460< /userid>
<Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
I have rented five or six times over the last seven years at Stevens Ave. Public Storage.  I have found this facility to be excellent.  The facility is clean, well maintained, secure, and easy to navigate with no surprises.

The staff has always been, professional, helpful, and friendly.  Juana the manager has been there for several years and has always been very enjoyable to work with.

Based on my consistently good experiences at the Stevens Avenue location, I would not hesitate to check with Public Storage first if I would ever need to rent at another location.

Customers should know that Public Storage does require renters insurance with the storage facility address listed as an insured location.  You can either buy insurance there, or arrange for it with your homeowners insurance.

Last time I priced rental coverage with my homeowners insurance, it saved me $5.00 dollars over the insurance sold at Public Storage for a short-term rental.   I just bought the public storage insurance, because I did not want to spend a 1/2 hour more on the phone with my insurance agency answering policy questions.   For longer term rentals, you may be able to save more money by adding the rental location to your home owners policy.

You will also need a Public Storage approved lock.   One of their approved locks is a round shielded shackle padlock.   They sell them for $15 on Amazon.  I bought mine at Public Storage years ago, and don't remember what I paid for it.   I think it was within a couple dollars of the Amazon price though.  [Update] Actually, I just look on the PS website and saw that their locks are a couple bucks cheaper than Amazon!

It is also very easy to reserve units online.  I have done this almost every time I have rented with them.  They have a variety of incentives on various sizes of storage lockers.  Do the math and you can find which incentive works best for your anticipated rental term.

While I have not rented with any other company, over the years I have occasionally shopped the competition, and also have gone with friends to their storage rental facilities.   I have never come across another company that offers more value than Public Storage.

I do not hesitate to recommend Public Storage.   For my needs their combination of location, facilities, and price is unbeatable.<//Review>

<user>112866712547314146758< /user><Name>nineironputt<//Name><date>1562340490899<//date>< Rating>
4</Rating>
<text>While visiting family in the area we all decided to give this place a spin. Everyone had a good time especially my son. Wait time was minimal and I was pleasantly surprised to see the track manager take my son out and teach him about cornering, braking etc. before the adults were unleashed. At the end of the race he even made the adults park and allowed my son to finetune his newfound skills for a bit with no one on the track.

If I was to give any negative feedback it would be the "throttling" of the karts. I came around a corner and was doing great suddenly our karts were all throttled down. A few moments later everyone was back up to speed except for mine. I thought did I hit something and was being penalized? I was nowhere near any walls or anyone when coming through the corner so that didn't make any sense. The only part that bugged me was I was left in this throttled state for well over a minute.  I then was able to get going again only to have it happen one more time.

Expensive and unappealing to have this sort of thing happen especially for no reason. I could see if I was bumping or hitting walls but that wasn't the case here. Even after the race the group that was with me made comments about my kart being throttled for so long and informing me that they too didn't see anything enforceable for the throttling.

Overall good fun, a little expensive but that's to be expected for these kinds of things.< /text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN7kIxdu1d6U-zKXemZxG8g8efwedd6doRMLUfu=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures><Resp>{'time': 1562636836384, 'text': "We're happy to accommodate for everyone on the track, and it's good to hear that your son got to try out some things he learned!
